SELECT "t"."Id", "t"."Author", "t"."Description", "t"."Name", "c"."id", "c"."BookId", "c"."BooksId", "c"."description", "c"."name"
FROM (
    SELECT "b"."Id", "b"."Author", "b"."Description", "b"."Name"
    FROM "Books" AS "b"
    WHERE "b"."Id" = @__Bookid_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS "t"
